10/10/2024, 23:13 - Matt Viney: With regards to your mates… Where abouts in Mumbai are they going to be staying? Either way, sharing thoughts that are on top of my mind… 

For food: 
1.⁠ ⁠Gaylord (Please ignore the cheeky colonial name) 😂 absolutely fabulous Indian & continental cuisine. 
2.⁠ ⁠⁠for bars there are many around Colaba causeway and Bandra. Worth checking out Yatch bar in bandra (we shot THE LIFT BOY there). Yatch is very basic but has its own charm & vibe. 
3.⁠ ⁠⁠I am sure they will hit the usual tourist spots like Queens Necklace/Marine Drive, Gateway of India, Taj Mahal Palace Hotel in Colaba, CST Train Station, Bandra Worli Sealink, Dharavi Slums (Slumdog Millionaire was shot there), Hanging Gardens, etc. 
4.⁠ ⁠⁠In terms of Malls: There is Jio World Drive in Bandra Kurla Complex and Jio World Plaza again in BKC (Bandra Kurla Complex). Then there is Palladium mall in Lower Parel. 
5.⁠ ⁠⁠In terms of cultural centres there is NMACC (Nita Mukesh Ambani Cultural Centre) and NCPA. Worth visiting both places. 
6.⁠ ⁠⁠If possible it’s worth having a good meal at Peshawari a restaurant at ITC Grand Maratha which is near the international airport. Absolutely splendid Indian food. 

Hope these recommendations help. Wishing them a splendid & safe trip. Cheers Matt 🥂

01/05/2025, 21:15 - Gupta: @13135550002 what's the opposite of out?
01/05/2025, 21:15 - Meta AI: The opposite of "out" can vary depending on the context in which it's used. Here are some possible antonyms:

- *Direction:*
    - *In*: When "out" indicates movement away from a place, "in" can be a suitable opposite, as in "going out" versus "coming in".
- *Visibility or Presence:*
    - *In*: When "out" means something is visible or available, "in" can imply the opposite, such as "the sun is out" versus "the sun is in" (behind clouds).
    - *Inside*: This can also work as an opposite in certain contexts, like "staying in" instead of "going out".
- *Status or Condition:*
    - *In*: In some cases, "in" can be an antonym when describing someone's status or condition, such as "out of commission" versus "in working order".
    - *Available*: When "out" means something is unavailable, "available" or "in stock" can be suitable opposites.
- *Other Possible Antonyms:*
    - *Inside*: When "out" refers to something being outside a boundary or area.
    - *Aloud* doesn't directly oppose "out", but in contexts where "out" means aloud, a possible antonym could be *silent* or *quietly*.
    - *Inclusion*: When "out" is used in phrases like "out of," antonyms could be *in*, *within*, or *inside*, depending on the context ¹.

Some specific examples include ²:
- *Out* (away from a place) → *In* (toward a place)
- *Out* (visible or known) → *Hidden* or *Unknown*
- *Out* (unavailable) → *Available* or *In stock*

Keep in mind that the best antonym will depend on how "out" is being used in a sentence or context.

Austin Pato - the spy who shouted at me!

An intriguing mission for all special agents at last night's Latch, as what looked liked two evenly pitched teams served up a Thunderball of a game, that was eventually won by Darks. However, the contest arguably swung after 40 mins when Mate sprained his ankle (in a very non-Bond unheroic way...being hit by the ball!). This allowed Darks to string together a succession of strikes that ultimately led to that sacred 007 goal difference for a 0.5pt bonus. 

The big winner in all of it was ABC, who not only finds himself at the TNF summit, but also headed straight off after the match to make a 9.15pm showing of the latest Bond movie. The fact he went there WITHOUT showering means there will have been a serious lack of re-Spectre from fellow film watchers sat near him in the cinema! 

The overriding theme of the game was certainly Pato's Goldfinger wagging at his fellow Whites, that brought a few frustrated responses from his team mates. The burly goal getter, with his licence to shoot on sight in full working order, took advantage of some odd job goalkeeping from the Darks to keep his team in touch. But when the match turned, along with Mate's ankle, Kabbadi and Nick eased the Darks home to leave living daylights in the final score line. 

For your eyes only that played last night, who was your man of the match? 

And for everyone that wants to die another day...who is in next week?
